### 10. 具有身份和表情锁定的高保真自拍

**Author**: [Dan Reed](https://x.com/daaaaanc)  **Date**: 2026-02-02  **Language**: en

> 一个高度技术性的提示，模拟原始、高保真度的 iPhone 17 Pro 自拍。它使用“身份锁定”（Identity Lock）和“表情同步”（Expression Sync）来确保面部几何结构、特定解剖特征（如痣）以及参考图像中的表情的绝对复制，同时详细描述表皮物理和纺织品结构，以实现超现实的效果。

![具有身份和表情锁定的高保真自拍](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1770100819695_ayuzxu_HAKodgAXMAApVIr.jpg)
![具有身份和表情锁定的高保真自拍](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1770100819453_9ciq0v_HAKodf9XMAUTACS.jpg)
![具有身份和表情锁定的高保真自拍](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1770100819517_7ud3zh_HAKodgEXMAA03rS.jpg)

```
(9;16). Raw high-fidelity photograph, iPhone 17 Pro simulation, 24mm wide focal length, f/2.4 aperture for deep focus with natural fall-off, authentic digital grain, high-angle POV selfie perspective.

Identity Lock: Absolute inheritance of facial geometry coordinates from Image A. Almond-shaped eyes with dense volumetric lash definition, specific lip symmetry with soft satin hydration, and the distinct pigmented mole located at the right nasolabial coordinate. Hair is {argument name="hair color" default="raven-black"}, straight, shoulder-length with a sharp center part and natural volume framing the face.
Bio-Fidelity: Epidermal physics featuring visible micro-pores on the nose, fine vellus hair along the jawline, and realistic skin texture across the shoulders and décolletage.
Expression Sync: Expression Lock—replicate the intense upward-tilted gaze, slight chin-down posture, and relaxed neutral pout from Image B.

Outfit & Physicality:

Technical Description: Structured strapless technical corset top in deep {argument name="top color" default="espresso brown"} with centered vertical ruching and a sweetheart neckline.
Textile Architecture: High-tensile fabric-to-skin compression physics; visible elasticized horizontal banding and micro-pleats in the ruched center section.
Anatomical Volume: Hyper-defined silhouette with maximum anatomical emphasis on the décolletage, clavicle definition, and bust geometry; apply the 20% over-description for natural anatomical ratio definition.
Pose & Interaction:

Geometry: High-angle selfie geometry; torso angled 15 degrees with the right shoulder pulled slightly back to emphasize the neckline.
Articulation: Realistic skeletal structure of the collarbones (clavicles) and neck tendons under the skin; natural skin-fold physics at the armpit-to-garment junction.
Environment & Lighting:

Atmosphere: Domestic indoor apartment setting; soft-diffused overhead ambient lighting with a slight 4500K neutral-warm bloom from a ceiling source.
Background Integrity: Pixel-perfect inventory of a high-pile cream-colored shag rug, a white paneled interior door on the left, a black ergonomic desk chair in the background, and a bed with a grey and white patterned duvet.
Shadow Ray-Tracing: Soft ambient occlusion shadows in the garment folds and under the jawline; realistic depth-mapping of the subject against the complex background textures.

**Author**: [Dan Reed](https://x.com/daaaaanc)  **Date**: 2026-02-02  **Language**: en

> 一个极其详细、技术性的提示，旨在生成一张模拟 iPhone 17 Pro 闪光灯摄影的原始、高保真肖像。它使用“身份锁定”（Identity Lock）和“表情同步”（Expression Sync）来精确复制外部参考（隐含的 A 和 B）的面部特征和表情，重点关注表皮物理、照明（硬闪光）和解剖体积。

![高保真闪光自拍肖像提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1770100797300_yey1qs_HAKjbqHXIAA67GZ.jpg)

```
(9:16). Raw high-fidelity photograph, iPhone 17 Pro simulation, 35mm portrait focal length, f/1.8 aperture for shallow depth of field, authentic digital grain and high-contrast front-facing flash photography aesthetics.

Identity Lock: Absolute inheritance of facial geometry coordinates from Image A. Almond-shaped eyes with extreme volumetric lash density, specific lip symmetry with high-gloss hydration, and the distinct pigmented mole located at the right nasolabial coordinate. Hair is raven-black, straight, shoulder-length with a sharp center part and natural movement.
Bio-Fidelity: Epidermal physics featuring visible micro-pores, fine vellus hair along the jawline, and high-intensity specular highlights on the forehead and cheeks from the flash source.
Expression Sync: Expression Lock—replicate the direct-to-lens gaze, 15-degree head tilt, and relaxed neutral pout with emphasized philtrum geometry from Image B.

Outfit & Physicality:

Technical Description: Strapless technical compression-fit tube top in matte obsidian black, featuring a scalloped floral lace-trim overlay at the upper hem.
Textile Architecture: High-tensile fabric-to-skin tension; visible lace weave patterns and elasticized structural seaming.
Anatomical Volume: Hyper-defined silhouette with maximum anatomical emphasis on the décolletage and bust geometry; apply the 20% over-description for natural anatomical ratio definition.
Accessories: 1mm silver micro-link chain with a centered teardrop-shaped crystal pendant.
Pose & Interaction:

Geometry: Medium-close portrait perspective; torso angled slightly away while the head turns toward the lens; prominent collarbone (clavicle) and shoulder-joint definition.
Articulation: Natural shoulder elevation to frame the face; realistic skin-texture transitions at the underarm and neck.
Environment & Lighting:

Atmosphere: Dimly lit domestic bedroom environment; dominated by a powerful, hard-light front-facing flash creating sharp contrast.
Background Integrity: Pixel-perfect inventory of a white-on-white textured duvet with organic fabric folds, a dark-stained wood-grain headboard, and neutral-toned wall surfaces.
Shadow Ray-Tracing: Hard-edged drop shadow cast directly behind the subject onto the background; deep ambient occlusion in the folds of the black garment.
```

### 22. 自上而下的电影感超现实主义肖像，带阴影映射

**Author**: [Vivek HY](https://x.com/Vivekhy)  **Date**: 2026-02-02  **Language**: en

> 一个高度技术化的 JSON 提示，用于以俯视角度生成安娜·德·阿玛斯（Ana de Armas）的电影感超现实肖像。它要求“解剖学身份锁定”（Anatomical_Identity_Lock），并指定独特的照明结构，包括柔和的自然阳光和阴影映射，将垂直和网格状图案投射到拍摄对象的面部和肩部。

```

Canvas: vertical poster, aspect ratio 2:3 (e.g. 4000×6000 px). High-res, photoreal, print-quality (minimum 300 DPI).
Composition: keep the ship’s bow centered and dominating the lower two-thirds; keep the couple faded and large in the top third as in the uploaded image (overlay/blend). Do not move or re-pose subjects.
Lighting & mood: cinematic golden-hour rim light on faces, soft warm highlights, cool deep shadows on the hull; strong contrast with gentle atmospheric mist; subtle film grain and slight vignette for vintage cinematic look.
Color grade: warm skin highlights, slightly desaturated midtones, deep navy/charcoal hull, soft cyan sky with white cloud details; natural skin texture preserved (no smoothing).
Ship details: maintain the bow’s perspective and railing lines; add realistic water spray/splash at the hull base, small white foam particles; keep deck rail details sharp.

Effects/finishing: increase perceived sharpness on ship hull and title; keep couple slightly softer; apply subtle film grain, mild chromatic aberration, and filmic contrast curve.
Negative constraints: no additional people or logos, no modern artifacts (phones, text), no watermark, no unnatural skin smoothness, no heavy plastic look.
For img2img parameters (suggested): strength 0.35–0.55, preserve composition, seed optional for reproducibility. Output: 4000×6000 PNG, lossless.
Instruction to renderer: Use the uploaded photo as the primary source and only refine/augment per the above — do not replace or re-render faces or change the original pose/composition.

> 一个高度技术性的提示，用于生成一个 4 格分屏图像，同时保持角色一致性（类似 Billie Eilish）。它侧重于极致的超现实主义，具体说明了“皮肤学上的真实感”，包括可见的毛孔、汗毛和未经修饰的皮肤纹理，并结合了硬质影棚闪光灯照明和高端相机设备细节（Phase One XF IQ4，柯达 Portra 400 模拟）。

  "lighting_and_shot": {

    "camera_shot": "Medium-full shot, capturing the subject from the knees up. The angle is slightly elevated, looking down at the subject against the backdrop of the pool. ### 43. Nano Banana Pro 稳定输出提示策略

**Author**: [みやび｜AI最適ビジネス研究家](https://x.com/miyabi_foxx)  **Date**: 2026-02-02  **Language**: ja

> 这是一套全面的指南，包含 10 条指令和策略，旨在帮助您为 Nano Banana Pro (Gemini 3 Pro Image) 编写有效的提示词，以稳定输出并避免乱码。它强调切换到“思维模式”或“专业模式”，使用描述性语句而非关键词列表，明确指定主体/背景/氛围，并使用积极的语言和英文关键词来提升质量。

![Nano Banana Pro 稳定输出提示策略](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1770100855406_jd9nn5_HAJLel0bsAA7EV_.jpg)
![Nano Banana Pro 稳定输出提示策略](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1770100855391_f359q8_HAJLjUobUAATIW7.jpg)

```
①モードは必ず「思考」か「Pro」に切り替える（肌感では「思考」の方が良い）
②キーワード羅列ではなく「情景を文章で描写」する
③被写体・背景・雰囲気の3点をセットで指定
④一発で完璧を目指さず「段階的に修正」を重ねる
⑤否定表現を避け、肯定文で指示する
⑥画質キーワード（4K、high resolution）は英語で追加
⑦用途を冒頭に明記する（例：「{argument name="用途" default="提案書用の図解"}」）
⑧ネガティブプロンプトで不要な要素を除外
⑨複雑な編集は一度にやらず分割して進める
⑩よく使うプロンプトはテンプレート化して保存
```

[[AI Prompt Engineering]]

**Author**: [𝐖𝐄𝐎𝐋𝐘𝐀𝐑𝐀𝐍𝐆 (달밤)](https://x.com/weolyarang)  **Date**: 2026-02-02  **Language**: ko

> 一个为 Nano Banana Pro/Gemini 设计的多帧提示词，用于创建三帧低分辨率网络摄像头拼贴画，并带有电影胶片美学（Cinesteel 800T）。它严格要求使用上传的人脸照片，且不得改变人物特征、性别或年龄。它指定了背景（日式旅馆）、服装（根据性别选择浴衣或丝绸衬衫），以及每帧独特的表情姿势，包括特定的灯光效果（红光、运动模糊）。

![三格胶片拼贴提示（摄影师版本）](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1770100861837_2j761a_HAI9Sj4aIAArBuc.jpg)

```
첨부한 얼굴 사진을 그대로 사용해 세로형 3프레임 low-res 웹캠 콜라주를 만든다

얼굴 관련 절대 규칙:

얼굴은 절대 변형하지 않는다

이목구비 비율, 얼굴형, 눈 크기, 코, 입, 턱선을 그대로 유지한다

나이를 더 어려 보이게 하거나 귀엽게 미화하지 않는다

입력된 사진 속 인물의 성별을 절대 변경하지 않는다

새로운 인물(이성/동성)을 생성하지 않는다

헤어스타일:

원본 헤어스타일을 유지한다

길이, 가르마, 컬은 바꾸지 않는다

다만 자연스럽게 살짝 흐트러진 러프한 상태로만 연출한다

촬영 톤 & 색감 (레퍼런스 반영):

첨부한 레퍼런스 사진과 동일한 색감으로 표현한다

배경:

일본식 나무로 만들어진 료칸.

배경 디테일은 최소화

어둡고 흐린 상태 유지

의상 규칙 (입력 사진 기준):

입력된 사진이 여자일 경우 → 모든 프레임에서 검은색에 빨간색 꽃무늬가 그려진 {argument name="female attire" default="유카타"}

입력된 사진이 남자일 경우 → 모든 프레임에서 검은색 실크 와이셔츠에 {argument name="male attire" default="빨간 넥타이"}

1번째 프레임:

슬픈 영화속 주인공처럼 슬픈 표정

입가 근처에 손가락

2번째 프레임:

고개는 살짝 옆으로 돌리고

아름다운 옆라인을 보여주고

일상적인 셀피 느낌, 과한 포즈 금지

3번째 프레임:

따뜻하고 아름다운 미소

양손은 깍지를 껴서 턱을 괸다

감정은 차분하고 몽환적인 분위기

중요 추가 지침:

입력된 사진 속 인물 한 명만 사용한다

성별, 얼굴, 분위기를 바꾸지 않는다

스타일 변화는 조명, 색감, 노이즈, 효과에만 적용한다

모든 프레임에서 동일한 얼굴을 일관되게 사용한다

효과 관련 절대 규칙:

모든 프레임에서 동일한 cinesteel 800T film style, 시네마틱 광원효과로 조명을 넣는다.

효과 관련 절대 규칙:

모든 프레임에서 동일한 한쪽엔 레드조명 효과와 좌에서 우로 센스있는 모션블러 효과를 넣는다.
```

```
画面为左右对半分割构图，左半与右半清晰分界，整体对齐，呈现“概念图与落地实景”的对照效果。
左半部分为高度精细的现代极简建筑平面图插画，风格与参考图一致。俯视正投影的住宅布局，包含并清晰标注空间与动线：客厅，餐区，开放式厨房，卧室，玄关，走廊及流线，阳台或廊下空间，飘窗与窗洞位置。配色使用中性米色与暖灰，线条干净利落，轻微柔影与细腻材质纹理，室内设计方案展示质感，蓝图式平铺视觉，家具摆放可见且尺度准确。
右半部分为与左侧平面图同一客厅的超写实室内照片效果，空间比例与布局严格对应平面图。客厅包含弧形沙发组合，中央茶几，柔软地毯，温润木地板，中性墙面，大窗引入自然光。整体为现代温暖的居家风，泥土色系与柔和灯光，材质真实可触，细节有生活感但保持整洁克制。右侧呈现为室内真实摄影质感，清晰纹理与高分辨率细节。
风格与氛围为建筑可视化结合真实室内摄影，现代，温暖，优雅，专业设计工作室展示感，强调从方案到实景的对比表达。
光照与色彩要求：左侧为均匀平光与中性色，右侧为自然日光与柔和阴影及暖高光；两侧色彩保持统一的和谐关系。
镜头与技术要求：左侧为顶视正交视角，右侧为室内广角镜头的平视视角，画面清晰锐利，真实材质与细节丰富。
负面提示词：卡通风，细节粗糙，室内杂乱，户型与实景不匹配，比例失真，过强硬光，夸张饱和色，文字叠加，水印，logo，噪点，模糊。
```

[[Interior Design Visualization]]

> 一个结构化的 JSON 提示，用于生成 Polina Gagarina 的四格垂直拼贴画，风格为逼真的高端时尚杂志编辑。它要求保持她精确的面部特征（身份锁定），并描绘她在黄金时段，身穿淡粉色花卉长裙，置身于郁郁葱葱的地中海庄园花园中。

            "Front-facing medium shot",
            "Close-up portrait"
          ]
        }
      },

**Author**: [Zara](https://x.com/ZaraIrahh)  **Date**: 2026-02-02  **Language**: en

> 一个高度结构化的 JSON 提示，用于生成一张高端生活时尚杂志风格的垂直四图网格拼贴画。它描述了一位身穿粉色花卉长裙的女士在户外花园场景中，强调自然阳光、愉悦的表情以及多姿态下的清晰细节。

      "type": "photorealistic_lifestyle_fashion_collage"
    },
    "subject": {

        "Woman": "Use from the reference image",
        "likeness_era": "Modern lifestyle editorial"
      },

        "hair": {
          "color": "Dark brown",
          "style": "Long, loose, center-parted",
          "texture": "Straight to softly wavy, lightly wind-swept"
        },
        "expression": {
          "mood": "Joyful, playful, carefree",
          "details": "Soft smile, joyful laughter, confident relaxed expressions"
        },
        "pose": {
          "position": "Standing and moving naturally across multiple frames",
          "orientation": "Front-facing, rear three-quarter view, mid-movement, and close medium portrait poses"
        }
      },
      "attire_and_accessories": {
        "clothing": {
          "item": "Maxi dress",
          "color": "Soft pink",
          "style_details": [
            "Small red and green floral print",
            "Short puff sleeves",
            "Fitted bodice",
            "Flowing skirt silhouette"
          ],
          "fabric_texture": "Lightweight, airy, flowing fabric"
        },
        "jewelry": {
          "item": "Earrings",
          "metal": "Minimal neutral metal",
          "style": "Simple, understated design"
        },
        "additional_accessories": [
          "Light brown ankle boots",
          "Sunglasses worn in one frame"
        ]
      }
    },
    "environment": {
      "immediate_setting": {
        "location_type": "Outdoor garden and landscaped estate grounds",
        "era_vibe": "Romantic countryside resort atmosphere",
        "interior_details": {
          "elements": [

            "Trees surrounding the grounds"
          ]
        }
      },
      "view_through_window": {

          "Distant mountains",
          "Clear blue sky",
          "Lush greenery"
        ]
      }
    },
    "photographic_execution": {
      "style": "High-end lifestyle fashion editorial photography",
      "quality": "High-resolution imagery with crisp subject detail",

### 111. 以人为本的永恒街头摄影

**Author**: [Özge Döner](https://x.com/astronomerozge1)  **Date**: 2026-02-01  **Language**: en

> 一个用于生成以人为中心的街头摄影的提示，营造出一种宁静、永恒的氛围，强调受控的调色板（深红色、暖橙色、泥土绿）和柔和的方向性照明，同时明确使用负面提示来避免人工 HDR 或塑料感。

![以人为本的永恒街头摄影](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1770014670895_z1zsj7_HAF4ogvXAAAAgZ3.jpg)

### 121. 丰腴海滩斜倚姿势，伴随刺眼阳光

### 163. 豪华东京酒店浴室肖像提示

**Author**: [Javeriya 🇺🇸](https://x.com/JadoonKhan281)  **Date**: 2026-02-01  **Language**: en

> 一个详细的 JSON 提示，用于生成一张在东京豪华酒店浴室中，一位女性的超写实肖像。它指定了 35mm 胶片美学、暖色钨丝灯照明，以及一件带有精致日式刺绣的黑色丝绸和服。

{
  "image_generation_request": {
    "title": "Cozy Tokyo Hotel Portrait",
    "version": "2.1",
    "mode": "photorealistic_portrait",
    "reference_settings": {
      "use_reference_image": true,
      "reference_type": "face_likeness",
      "strength": 0.85
    },

      "subject": {
        "description": "Precise facial likeness of the blonde woman from the reference, with clear, glowing skin.",
        "pose": "Standing centered, facing the camera, holding a white ceramic mug with both hands.",
        "expression": "Warm, genuine smile with eyes looking toward the camera."
      },
      "attire": {
        "item": "Black silk kimono robe with a deep V-neckline.",
        "details": "Intricate Japanese floral and koi carp embroidery in gold and red tones."
      },
      "environment": {
        "location": "Luxurious, dimly lit hotel bathroom in Tokyo.",
        "background_elements": "Large mirrors on both sides reflecting the subject's back and the warm room lighting; marble countertop and chrome faucet visible.",
        "atmosphere": "Quiet, cozy late-night vibe with visible steam rising from the mug."
      },
      "lighting": {
        "type": "Soft, warm tungsten lighting from a wall sconce.",
        "effects": "Gentle shadows, cinematic glow on the hair, and soft highlights on the face."
      },
      "technical_photography": {
        "camera": "35mm film photography style",
        "lens_settings": "f/1.8 aperture, shallow depth of field, sharp focus on the face.",
        "texture": "Fine film grain, natural skin textures, high dynamic range."
      }
    },
    "concatenated_prompt": "Photorealistic portrait of a blonde woman with a precise facial likeness to the reference, smiling warmly at the camera. She is standing in a dimly lit, luxury Tokyo hotel bathroom, holding a white ceramic mug with steam rising from it. She wears a black silk kimono with gold and red floral embroidery. The background features large mirrors reflecting her figure and the warm glow of a wall sconce. 35mm film aesthetic, f/1.8 aperture, soft cinematic lighting, warm tungsten tones, fine grain, ultra-detailed, high-end fashion editorial style.",
    "negative_prompt": "bright daylight, harsh shadows, fluorescent light, sad expression, distorted hands, blurry face, low resolution, cartoonish, messy environment, direct harsh flash.",
    "parameters": {
      "aspect_ratio": "2:3",
      "sampler": "DPM++ 2M Karras",
      "steps": 30,
      "cfg_scale": 7.5
    }
  }
}

### 200. 简单的图片集成提示

**Author**: [七表哥](https://x.com/seven_cuz)  **Date**: 2026-02-01  **Language**: en

> 一个基本的提示，指示 AI 将上传的图片（大概是人物和衣服）整合到一张图片中，显示主体坐在一张纯色沙发上，置身于一个温暖舒适的房间里，画面比例为 9:16。

![简单的图片集成提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1770014674479_8pbgkg_HADBxQZbkAAqKTl.jpg)
![简单的图片集成提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1770014674493_30bxo0_HADB1uDbEAQPxTT.jpg)

```
Integrate the uploaded pictures into one in a 9:16 format: Sitting on a solid-colored sofa in a warm and cozy room, posing in a delicate manner.
```

[[9:16 Vertical Format]]

---
